<gmapID>0x80945d2fd8ef9b17:0xe2a98a8ee780cbf4<//gmapID>< review>
Okay, I'll be honest. I'm not a huge Chinese food guy. But we were invited to an affair here, so I had no choice. I'll say this for the place: If you don't know it's there, you won't likely find it. It's tucked away back in a corner of a strip mall. That's not an auspicious indication of quality, but they seem to have overcome that location obscurity and have a following I'm told. Service was spotty. Good at first, and then, as they got busier not so good. I don't think it would be fair for me to evaluate the dishes, as I'm not a Chinese afficionado. In our party there were 11 people, and each chose a dish that they wanted and it was served family style. So, I did have the opportunity to sample several dishes. However, that said, I do not eat meat, so that limited my samplings. Prices are not real cheap, but that's to be expected if you're going to expect high quality.< /review>

<Name>Nevin Hindiyeh</Name>< Review>
This place is a Fresno gem. Great food and great service. Their lunch specials are a steal running at about $11 for soup, salad, chicken appetizer, egg roll, and rice or chow mein. We generally ask to substitute a second egg roll for the chicken appetizer and get half chow mein half fried rice. Their family dinners are also amazing. We love the sizzling rice soup and their strawberry prawns. Mmmmm.</Review>

<Time>1532578848934< /Time><rate>2<//rate><Review>(Translated by Google) When this place is just open I almost the first customer to try their food. At that time all the dishes tastes good, nice and clean environment. I take too many pictures and public them on Google map, and write reviews for it. Some dishes taste good, but all American style Chinese food, too sweet for most Chinese guys. In recent year's I always came here to have meals when I pass by Fresno. Years after years, dishes taste change too much, not Change better but to worse I think. Like most restaurant, when their business becomes good they will pay little attention to their service and food. By the way, food is good at first but not now. Recommend two or three years before, but not recommended now.
For most Chinese restaurant they used somecheap tea give free tea for their customers, but right now, they also use cheapest tea but need customer to pay for the worst tested tea. Can't understand what's the manager's idea about it.
For the location is a little bit hard to find, it's located not besides the walkway, need go a little bit further from a ailse in the middle of the parking lot.

When the restaurant first opened, I was almost one of the first people to eat here. At the beginning, the taste and service of the food were still acceptable, but it was in line with American food tastes and was acceptable. You should know that there are not many Chinese food choices in Fresno! I come to eat here almost every year when I pass by, but the last time I feel I can‚Äôt eat anymore! The taste of the food is not good, and the service is not good anymore~ For the average Chinese restaurant, the tea made with the cheapest tea is usually provided for free, but there is even a charge now~ If possible, go Try other Chinese restaurants~

(Original)
When this place is just open I almost the first customer to try their food. At that time all the dishes tastes good, nice and clean environment. I take too many pictures and public them on Google map, and write reviews for it. Some dishes taste good, but all American style Chinese food, too sweet for most Chinese guys. In recent year's I always came here to have meals when I pass by Fresno. Years after years, dishes taste change too much, not Change better but to worse I think. Like most restaurant, when their business becomes good they will pay little attention to their service and food. By the way, food is good at first but not now. Recommend two or three years before, but not recommended now.
For most Chinese restaurant they used somecheap tea give free tea for their customers, but right now, they also use cheapest tea but need customer to pay for the worst tested tea. Can't understand what's the manager's idea about it.
For the location is a little bit hard to find, it's located not besides the walkway, need go a little bit further from a ailse in the middle of the parking lot.

< Text>
One of the newest Subways up here in Apple Valley. Seating and parking are minimal but the restaurant is new and it's a lot closer than any other subway for me. Apple pay is accepted here (and works). I've done app orders with the Subway app and everything worked very smoothly (don't wait in line, just tell them your name, and you're good). Staff know Spanish and were very patient with my mother in law (from Peru). This subway neighbors a Roundtable (Pizza), a yogurt shop, a fruit juice shop, and a T-Mobile. Starbucks is a minute walk south. There is very limited outdoor seating.<//Text>

Tried to make an online reservation, but it would only let us make one for the next day. Arrived later that afternoon & it was not half full yet.

Our server, Tess, was great! Kept her running with tea refills, always returned with a smile. Food was delicious & she almost convinced me to try the cauliflower burger (I know, sounds gross, maybe worth a try next time?).

Store was a little disappointing because the shirts we collect were no longer available (location-unique designs on back). But found another shirt that'd be a decent substitute. Worth returning to if we come this way again.

One recommendation - get the valet parking! Have the restaurant validate it & save several bucks over parking yourselves. Worth it!</review>

< Text>
I'm somewhat of a Hard Rock fan.  I try to visit one anytime I'm out of town.  I walked in and took a seat at the bar with 0 expectations outside of a meal and a drink.  I got more than that.  The good was good, drinks were good.  But let me tell you service was phenomenal.  I have never experienced bar service like this before.  The bartender was Kimbo Slice and not the late MMA fighter either.  This girl was amazing.  Friendly which should be an automatic for a bartender.   But also extremely attentive.  There was never a moment of trying to find the bartender yell for them try and get their attention.   She was on top of all her customers and made sure they got anything they needed.  I was impressed.  If you go here and sit at the bar and have Kimbo Slice as your bartender, you've hit the jackpot.</Text>

(Translated by Google) Anyone who has been to Universal Studios must also eat in hard rock.
The burger is the best I've ever had and the service is incredibly nice. It was my third time there and I still find it incredible. It is simply an experience to eat there. You should also take a photo from the balcony.

I can only recommend this restaurant!

<Time>1449510258398< /Time><rate>4</rate><Review>You might think Sushi in Del Mar is gonna be a costly endeavor and that you might be able to save some time and money by going a little further north to Solana, Encinitas or Carlsbad and in general you'd be right, but this unassuming spot barely looks like a sushi spot from the outside and actually that rusty gate from the grocery store next door probably scare people off. It's awesome to come here when it's slow, you get super fast and amazing food and during daytime they have a HH that's killer on the deals. Kai roll, sushi burrito, philly.

They serve a ton of regulars and most of the staff will remember you if you come in a lot. The service is great, but most of all from the chef's with their great flavor profiles, knife skills and recommendations.

They have some major price jumps between standard rolls and premium as well as for their MP items like Uni, Toro, etc. The salad pricing like wakame is a bit high. If you don't mind getting certain rolls the HH can be as inexpensive as any place around, but their quality will keep you coming back regardless of the price.

Found out about this place as they also own Nozomi in Carlsbad, another diamond in the rough. Urban, Balance and Flower Hill have brought a lot more attention to this side of the 5.

Their salmon tends to be firm, while their tuna I found soft. They use a lot of jalapeno, cream cheese and sriracha in their rolls. They perfectly don't over fry their shrimp, the unagi sauce is a bit of an overload and really sweet. I always ask to go easy on the crunchies if any at all.

I don't like the word fusion and you'll see it in the rest of their menu being that it's pretty limited on the back end, but the front chefs are great.< /Review><pictures>None< /pictures>< Resp>
None</Resp>

< Review>
My wife and I ordered teriyaki vegetables and sushi to-go and were relatively disappointed with our meal. The service we experienced was good and we received our to-go order quickly, but the sushi just wasn't that great. The teriyaki vegetables were amazing and we really enjoyed those, but the two sushi rolls we ordered were just mediocre. Part of our issue was that the soy sauce which was served with our sushi (in little to-go packets) was incredibly salty. Disgustingly so. It completely overwhelmed the flavor of the sushi, the ginger, and the wasabi sauce. We'll definitely be back for some more teriyaki vegetables and chicken, but next time we'll probably skip the sushi. On a side note the prices for a $$ location weren't too bad. You can purchase sushi rolls there for as low as $5.50-ish (for an 8-piece roll). More expensive rolls can run up to $15 for a 10 piece roll. The excellent teriyaki vegetables were $12 for a substantial serving.< /Review>
